 Indian national anthem 'jana Gana Mana
 
 
 ' ne mangalvaar ko sau saal puure kar liye
 This anthem composed by Kaviguru Rabindranath Tagore was sung for the first time at the Calcutta session of the Indian National Congress on this day in 1911
 antat: bharat kii swadhinata ke teen saal baad 24 janvari, 1950 ko samvidhan sabha ne is gaan ko aadhikarik taur par desh ke raashtragan ke rup main angikaar kiya
 The first five verses of this eulogy composed by Tagore in Sanskritistha Bangla were adopted as the national anthem
 ise prastut karne main 52 second lagate hai
 Tagore is said to have composed this poem in the coronation court of the British ruler George V
 kuch logon kaa maananaa he ki yah kavita jorge pancham kii prashasti main rachi gai thi, ishwar kii stuti main nahin
 Tagore, however, translated 'jana Gana Mana' into English as 'the morning song of India' which addressed God and the Motherland
 unhone is gaan ko andhra pradesh ke chitoor jile ke madanapalle kasbe main sangitabaddh kiya tha

 There is a demand to declare it a national disaster in view of the floods
 haalanki, kendriya mantri alphons kannanthanam ne kaha he ki aapadaa prabandhan kanoon 2005 main kisi aapadaa ko rashtriya aapadaa ghoshit karne kaa praavdhaan nahin he
 Let us know what is the difference between a national disaster and a serious disaster
 aapadaa kii paribhaashaapada prabandhan adhinium, 2005 ke mutabik 'aapadaa' kaa matlab hota he kisi bhi ilaake main prakritik yaa maanavajanit kaarnon se, yaa durghatana yaa upeksha kii vajah se ai aisi koi mahavipatti, anisht, tabaahi aadi jisase maanav jivan kii baari haani yaa sampatti ko baari nuksaan or vinaash, yaa paryaavaran ko baari kshati pahunche or yah itane bade paimaane par ho ki jisase sthaneey samudaay ke liye nipatna sambhav na ho
 Natural and man-made disasters: earthquakes, floods, landslides, cyclones, tsunamis, floods in urban areas, heatwaves etc

 jaise umdaa bhajan ko likhane vaale punjabi, urdu ke sufi sant darvesh shah hossain kii yaad main sahitya academy ne 'kahe hossain fakir sai da: shah hossain' naamak ek parisamvaad kaa aayojan rajdhani sthit rabindra bhawan sabhaagaar main kiya, jisamen punjab or dilli ke punjabi or urdu ke saath hi sufi santon par kaam kar chuke kai diggaj lekhakon ne hissaa liya
 Sahitya Akademi secretary k Srinivasrao started the program with his welcome address
 unhone kaha ki bharat sufi santon or bhakt kaviyon kii bhoomi he
 The academy is feeling content with organizing this seminar centered on the great Sufi saint Darvesh Shah Hussain
 isliye bhi ki jab puri duniya nafrat, aatank or atibhautikatawaad se grast he, tab darvesh shah hossain jaise sufi santon kii vaniyan hi hamen prem, sadbhaav or santosh ke raste par laa sakati hai
 Rao said that Shah Hussain was a contemporary of Akbar and Jahangir
 shah hossain ke guru arjunadev ji or chajju bhakt ke saath bahut achche sambandh the
 Punjabi has a particular poetic-type - 'quite'
 darvesh shah hossain ko isaki shuruyaat karne vaala bhi mana jaataa he
 His composition has a sense of inner rhythm and spirituality
 academy ke sachiv ne kaha ki shah hossain ke kaafiyon main darshanik prem kii ati ucch bhaavana he, jo sabhi dharmon, panthon, jatiyon or har bandhan ko todakar apane aradhy se milane kii utkar ichha se bhari hui he
 It is this spirit which elevates a man from his position and he starts loving the human being
 shah hossain apane dehavsaan ke samay tak ekanishtha bhav se sabake man main prem kii alakh jagaate rahe the
 Vanita, the convenor and noted poetess of the Punjabi Consultation Board of Sahitya Akademi, in her opening statement introduced Shah Hussain's unique position in Punjabi literature and highlighted his 'coffee' characteristics
 unhone kaha ki punjabi sufi sant shah hossain ke kaafiyon ne punjab kii samskruti, sangeet, bhashaa or sabhyachaar ko shaamil kiya jiske kaaran vah har punjabi ke hriday main bas gai he
 Highlighting the spiritual personality and social coverage of Shah Hussain, the famous Punjabi scholar Sukhdev Singh Sirsa, president of the Punjabi Sahitya Academy, Ludhiana, said in his seed statement that Shah Hussain played a big role in establishing such an emotional connection between man and the divine That through which great humanity is born within the person
 shah hossain kii bhakthi or unki kafiyan jan-man main basii hui hai
 His association with society made his devotion liberal, tolerant and benevolent
 shimla vishvavidhyalay ke kulapati harmohinder singh bedi ne udghaatan satr main adhyakshiya vaktavy dete hue kaha ki shah hossain kii rachanaaen apane aradhy rupi priyatam ke prati ek bhaktapremi kii manuhaar, ulaahna or ragaatmakataa kaa ujjwal dastauez hai
 The more a person goes into the Sufi world, the more he associates with saints like Shah Hussain
 
 Aziz Hajini, convener of the Kashmiri Consultation Board of Sahitya Akademi and noted Kashmiri litterateur, presided over the first session on 'ranjha Mile Kittan Dhange' and spoke on the poetry of Shah Hussain
 unhone kaha ki shah hossain kii rachanaaon ke mul main punjabi ke logon kaa jazbaa, pyaar, laalasaa or pavitrataa he, jiske kaaran unki kafiyan lokgeeton ke rup main logon kii jubaan par chadh gayi,is satr main harbhajan singh bhaatia ne 'shah hossain da kalam: anubhav ate andaaz', mustaaq kadri ne 'tasawwuf shah hossain' tathaa ravel singh ne 'birahaa ate shah hossain' vishay par apane gambhir aalekh prastut kiye
 The theme of the second session, based on Sufi saint Darvesh Shah Hussain, was 'dard Vichhodhe Da Hall', presided over by noted Punjabi litterateur Sumail Singh Sidhu
 is satr main 'maai ni main kehnu aankhaan' vishay par punjabi yuva kavi or aalochak jagavinder jodha ne apana suchintit aalekh prastut kiya
 The program was conducted by Sneha Chaudhuri, the English editor of Sahitya Akademi

 ’ Kalabhairava Ashtami is the day on which you can appease the interview, you can ask for wishes
 yah din kaal kii puja kaa din hota he, is ashtami ko bhairav ashtami bhi kaha jaataa he
 Kalbhairava Ashtami is on Friday 14 November
 ashtami ke din punya tithi main vidhi-vidhaan se kii gai puja kalbhairav kaa vardaan hi nahin dilaati, balki aapaki samast manokamanaayon ko bhi puraa kar sakati he
 The meaning of Bhairav is to remove fear and fill the world
 aisa bhi kaha jaataa he ki bhairav shabd ke teen aksharon main brahma, vishnu or mahesh teenon kii shakti samahit he
 Bhairav is considered a follower of Shiva's Ganesha and Parvati
 hindu devataaon main bhairav kaa bahut hi mahatv he or bhairav ashtami ke din puja upasna se sabhi shatruon or paapi shaktiyon kaa naash hota he
 All kinds of sins, heat and suffering are removed
 manyata he ki is din vrath, shodshopchaar pujan karne se punya falon kaa prapti hoti he
 Kaal Bhairava is the incarnation of Shiva
 aughaddani kii tarah hi dani or vishaal hriday vaale hai bhairo baba
 On Kalabhairava Ashtami, Baba does welfare of devotees in every way
 is baar to kalbhairav ashtami or zyada vishesh ho gai he, kyonki is din kuch vishesh yoga bane hue hai
 Where Mercury is present in Libra on one side which is the sign of Venus, due to which Bhadra Yoga is being formed which is considered very auspicious
 panditon kii maane to is yoga ko grah pidaa nivaaran ke liye behad uttam mana jaataa he

 The no-confidence motion against the ruling Modi government at the Center will be discussed and voted on Friday
 modi sarkaar ke sava chaar saal main pehali baar vipaksh avishvaas prastaav laayaa he
 The government has more numbers than the majority figure, so it is convinced that this proposal is not successful
 vaise desh ke sansad ke itihaas main ab tak kareeb 26 baar avishvaas prastaav aae hai lekin do baar hi vipaksh ko isamen safalataa mili he
 The first motion of no confidence in the Indian Parliament came against the then Prime Minister Jawaharlal Nehru in 1963
 nehru ke khilaaf jebi kriplani ne avishvaas prastaav rakhaa tha
 JB Kripalani left the party and started the Kisan Mazdoor Praja Party, which later changed to the Praja Socialist Party in association with the Socialist Party, due to the Congress not being re-elected president
 praja socialist party ke tatkaaleen saansad jebi kriplani dwaara nehru sarkaar ke khilaaf laae gaye avishvaas prastaav ke paksh main 62 vot or virodh main 347 vot pade
 In this way, the motion of no confidence collapsed
 nehru ke nidhan ke baad desh ke pradhanmantri laal bahadur shastri bane
 During his three-year tenure, no confidence motion was brought by the opposition thrice, but not even once did the opposition succeed
 iske baad satta kii kaman indira gandhi ko mili
 Indira Gandhi completed Shastri's remaining term
 is dauraan unke khilaaf do baar prastaav laayaa gaya
 The most no-confidence motion in Indian parliamentary history has been faced by the Congress government led by Prime Minister Indira Gandhi
 indira gandhi ke khilaaf vipaksh 15 baar avishvaas prastavlaya, par ek bhi baar use kamyaabi nahin mili
 The record of presenting the highest no-confidence motion from the opposition is in the name of Jyoti Basu, the Communist Party of india-marxist MP
 unhone apane chaaron prastaav indira gandhi kii sarkaar ke khilaaf rakhe the
 The 1978 no-confidence motion of the opposition was successful for the first time in India's parliamentary history
 apatkaal ke baad hue chunaav main janata party ko bahumat mila or morarji desai pradhanmantri bane
 During the tenure of Morarji Desai government, a motion of no confidence was brought against him twice
 pehle prastaav se unhen koi pareshaani nahin hui, lekin 1978 main duusari baar laae gaye avishvaas prastaav main unki sarkaar ke ghatak dalon main aapasi matbhed the
 As soon as his defeat was realized, Morarji Desai resigned before the division of votes
 laal bahadur shastri kii tarah narsimha raav kii sarkaar ko bhi teen baar avishvaas prastaav kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 In 1993, Narasimha Rao was able to beat the no-confidence motion against his government
 narsimha sarkaar ke khilaaf aae avishvaas prastaav ke voting main 14 vot ke antar se sarkaar bachi
 However, he was also accused of luring the mps of Jharkhand Mukti Morcha to save his government
 endie sarkaar ke purv pradhanmantri atal bihari vaajapeyi ne vipaksh main rahete hue do baar avishvaas prastaav pesh kiye
 When Vajpayee became Prime Minister himself, he too faced a no-confidence motion twice
 inamen se pehali baar to wo sarkaar nahin bachaa paae lekin duusari baar vipaksh ko unhone maat de di
 In 1999, the Atal Bihari Vajpayee government faced a no-confidence motion by withdrawing the support of Jayalalithaa's party
 tab vaajapeyi sarkaar 1 vot ke andar se haar gai thi
 He had already resigned before voting
 iske baad 2003 main vaajapeyi ke khilaaf laae avishvaas prastaav ko endie ne aaraam se vipaksh ko voton kii ginati main haraa diya tha
 The NDA got 312 votes while the opposition was reduced to 186 votes
